      [@CLASS        ]
          @@doc : - Classes and Method Resolution Order
         |--  [Class ComplexWarning]
                 |--  MRO - Class Member Resolution Order:
                         |--  <class 'numpy.core.numeric.ComplexWarning'>
                         |--  <class 'RuntimeWarning'>
                         |--  <class 'Warning'>
                         |--  <class 'Exception'>
                         |--  <class 'BaseException'>
                         |--  <class 'object'>
                 |--  [  getset_descriptor  ]:
                         |--  args
                 |--  [  method_descriptor  ]:
                         |--  with_traceback
         |--  [Class DataSource]
                 |--  MRO - Class Member Resolution Order:
                         |--  <class 'numpy.lib._datasource.DataSource'>
                         |--  <class 'object'>
                 |--  [  function  ]:
                         |--  _cache (['self', 'path'])
                         |--  _findfile (['self', 'path'])
                         |--  _isurl (['self', 'path'])
                         |--  _iswritemode (['self', 'mode'])
                         |--  _iszip (['self', 'filename'])
                         |--  _possible_names (['self', 'filename'])
                         |--  _sanitize_relative_path (['self', 'path'])
                         |--  _splitzipext (['self', 'filename'])
                         |--  abspath (['self', 'path'])
                         |--  exists (['self', 'path'])
                         |--  open (['self', 'path', 'mode'])
         |--  [Class MachAr]
                 |--  MRO - Class Member Resolution Order:
                         |--  <class 'numpy.core.machar.MachAr'>
                         |--  <class 'object'>
                 |--  [  function  ]:
                         |--  _do_init (['self', 'float_conv', 'int_conv', 'float_to_float', 'float_to_str', 'title'])
         |--  [Class ModuleDeprecationWarning]
                 |--  MRO - Class Member Resolution Order:
                         |--  <class 'numpy.ModuleDeprecationWarning'>
                         |--  <class 'DeprecationWarning'>
                         |--  <class 'Warning'>
                         |--  <class 'Exception'>
                         |--  <class 'BaseException'>
                         |--  <class 'object'>
                 |--  [  getset_descriptor  ]:
                         |--  args
                 |--  [  method_descriptor  ]:
                         |--  with_traceback
         |--  [Class PackageLoader]
                 |--  MRO - Class Member Resolution Order:
                         |--  <class 'numpy._import_tools.PackageLoader'>
                         |--  <class 'object'>
                 |--  [  function  ]:
                         |--  _execcmd (['self', 'cmdstr'])
                         |--  _format_titles (['self', 'titles', 'colsep'])
                         |--  _get_doc_title (['self', 'info_module'])
                         |--  _get_info_files (['self', 'package_dir', 'parent_path', 'parent_package'])
                         |--  _get_sorted_names (['self'])
                         |--  _init_info_modules (['self', 'packages'])
                         |--  _obj2repr (['self', 'obj'])
                         |--  error (['self', 'mess'])
                         |--  get_pkgdocs (['self'])
                         |--  log (['self', 'mess'])
                         |--  warn (['self', 'mess'])
         |--  [Class RankWarning]
                 |--  MRO - Class Member Resolution Order:
                         |--  <class 'numpy.lib.polynomial.RankWarning'>
                         |--  <class 'UserWarning'>
                         |--  <class 'Warning'>
                         |--  <class 'Exception'>
                         |--  <class 'BaseException'>
                         |--  <class 'object'>
                 |--  [  getset_descriptor  ]:
                         |--  args
                 |--  [  method_descriptor  ]:
                         |--  with_traceback
         |--  [Class Tester]
                 |--  MRO - Class Member Resolution Order:
                         |--  <class 'numpy.testing.nosetester.NoseTester'>
                         |--  <class 'object'>
                 |--  [  function  ]:
                         |--  _get_custom_doctester (['self'])
                         |--  _show_system_info (['self'])
                         |--  _test_argv (['self', 'label', 'verbose', 'extra_argv'])
                         |--  bench (['self', 'label', 'verbose', 'extra_argv'])
                         |--  prepare_test_args (['self', 'label', 'verbose', 'extra_argv', 'doctests', 'coverage'])
                         |--  test (['self', 'label', 'verbose', 'extra_argv', 'doctests', 'coverage', 'raise_warnings'])
                 |--  [  list  ]:
                         |--  excludes
         |--  [Class VisibleDeprecationWarning]
                 |--  MRO - Class Member Resolution Order:
                         |--  <class 'numpy.VisibleDeprecationWarning'>
                         |--  <class 'UserWarning'>
                         |--  <class 'Warning'>
